GOVERNMENT GAZETTE 
EXTRAORDINARY	
PUBLISHED BY AUTHORITY
THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION, CHEPAUK, CHENNAI
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION (1) OF SECTION 15 OF THE TAMIL NADU HIGHWAYS ACT, 2001 
(LA- V(1)/11902013/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-1)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be acquired 
for Highways Department for the purpose to “Widening of four lanes to six lanes from Thirunindravur to Padi in Km 59/6 
to 81/6 of Chennai – Thiruthani – Renigunda Road (SHU-148)” in Vilingiyambakkam Village, Avadi Taluk of Tiruvallur 
District and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be 
paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Chief Engineer (C & M), Highways Department. The following notice 
is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), 
 the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 3950 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for “Widening of four lanes to six lanes from Thirunindravur to 
Padi in Km 59/6 to 81/6 of Chennai – Thiruthani – Renigunda Road (SHU-148)” at Vilingiyambakkam Village, Avadi 
Taluk of Tiruvallur District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer, (LA-2) Highways, Tiruvallur 
and in the office of the Special Tahsildar (LA-2), Highways,Unit – III, Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during 
office hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
(LA- V(1)/11903948/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-2)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below are acquired 
for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation 
of Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy” at No No.50.Pulivai Village, Uthiramerur Taluk, 
Kancheepuram District and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Managing Director, Tamil Nadu Road Development 
Company Limited, Chennai Valayakaranai to Manampathi Road having considering the cause shown by the owner or 
other persons having interest on such lands if any, as the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice under 
sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 5690 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor 
of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation of Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy” 
at No.50.Pulivai Village, Uthiramerur Taluk, Kancheepuram District.
The Plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), Highways 
Kancheepuram and Office of the Special Tahsildar (LA) Highways, Unit – 6, Kancheepuram may be inspected on any 
day during office hours.

Total extent to be acquired 5075 Sq.mtrs
(LA-V(1)/11902166/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-4)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below are acquired 
for Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation of 
Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy” at No.02.Palur “B” Village, Chengalpattu Taluk & 
District and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be paid 
out of the funds controlled and managed by the Highways Department after having considering the cause shown by 
the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice 
under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 138249 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor 
of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation of Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy” 
in No.02.Palur “B” Village, Chengalpattu Taluk & District.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
The Plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), Highways 
Chengalpattu (Chengalpattu Sub-Collector Office Back side) may be inspected on any day during office hours.

23
(LA-V(1)/111939232/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-5)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below are 
acquired under the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase for 
"Formation of Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy" at No.58. Neyyadupakkam Village, 
Uthiramerur Taluk, Kancheepuram District and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be 
awarded for the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Managing Director, Tamil Nadu Road 
Development Company Limited. Chennai Valayakaranal to Manampathi Road having considering the cause shown by 
the owner or other persons having interest on such lands if any, as the case may be, do hereby publish the following 
notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), 
the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 922 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor 
of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase I for "Formation of Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy" 
at No.58. Neyyadupakkam Village, Uthiramerur Taluk, Kancheepuram District
The Plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), Highways 
Kancheepuram and Office of the Special Tahsildar (LA) Highways, Unit-5, Kancheepuram may be inspected on any 
day during office hours.

35792
Total extent to be acquired 35792 Sq.mtrs
(LA-V(1)/11903775/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-8)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below are acquired for 
the Highways purpose to wit for “Strengthening and Widening SH -113A Poonamallee – Kundrathur – Pallavaram 
Road at Km 5/2 – 12/0” at No No.69.Manancheri Village, Kundrathur Taluk, Kancheepuram District and it having already 
been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and 
managed by the Divisional Engineer (Highways), Construction and Maintenance, Chennai Poonamalle – Kundrathur – 
Pallavaram Road having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands 
if any, as the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil 
Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 6938 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for the Highways purpose to wit for “Strengthening and Widening 
SH -113A Poonamallee – Kundrathur – Pallavaram Road at Km 5/2 – 12/0” at No No.69.Manancheri Village, 
Kundrathur Taluk, Kancheepuram District.
The Plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), Highways 
Kancheepuram and Office of the Special Tahsildar (LA) Highways, Unit – 3, Kancheepuram may be inspected on any 
day during office hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
37
(LA- V(1)/12015982/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-9)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be acquired 
for Highways Department for the purpose to “Widening from Intermediate Lane to Four Lane and Strengthening 
at Km 0/0 – 2/2 of GNT Road to Chinnambedu Road (Via) Chinnambedu Colony and Km 2/2 – 3/0 of New 
Alternative Road (PP Road – Pettai)” in Durainallur & Chinnambedu - I Villages, Ponneri Taluk of Tiruvallur District 
and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out 
of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer (C & M), Tiruvallur after having considering the cause 
shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following 
notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
 NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 20843 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for “Widening from Intermediate Lane to Four Lane and 
Strengthening at Km 0/0 – 2/2 of GNT Road to Chinnambedu Road (Via) Chinnambedu Colony and Km 2/2 
– 3/0 of New Alternative Road (PP Road – Pettai)” at Durainallur & Chinnambedu - I Villages, Ponneri Taluk of 
Tiruvallur District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer, (LA-1) Highways, Tiruvallur and in 
the office of the Special Tahsildar (LA), Highways, Unit – I, Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.

Sq.mtrs.,
Total Extent to be acquired 20843 Sq.mtrs.
(LAV(1)/12123079/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-10)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation of 
Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy” in No.82.Neerkundram Village located in Uthiramerur 
Taluk, Kancheepuram District and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
land is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Managing Director, Tamil Nadu Road Development 
Company Limited, Chennai Valayakaranai to Manampathi Road having considering the cause shown by the owner or 
other persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub 
section 1 of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act No. 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section 1 of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu is hereby acquires the Wet and Dry lands specified in the schedule below and measuring an extent 
of 38274 Sq.mtrs of lands in No.82.Neerkundram Village located in Uthiramerur Taluk, Kancheepuram District and 
these to the same, a little more or less needed for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor 
of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation of Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy”. 


	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
45
The plan of the lands are kept in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer (LA), Highways, Kancheepuram 
and Special Tahsildar (LA), Highways Unit- 5, Kancheepuram may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(LAV(1)/12128939/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-11)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor of Cheyyar SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation of 
Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy” in No.81.Padur Village in Uthiramerur Taluk, Kancheepuram 
District and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the land is to be paid 
out of the funds controlled and managed by the Managing Director, Tamil Nadu Road Development Company Limited, 
Chennai Valayakaranai to Manampathi Road having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having 
interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub section 1 of Section 15 
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act No. 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub Section 1 of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu is hereby acquires the Wet and Dry lands specified in the schedule below and measuring an 
extent of 150914 Sq.mtrs of lands in No.81.Padur Village in Uthiramerur Taluk, Kancheepuram District and these to the 
same, a little more or less needed for the Highways purpose to wit to Development of Industrial Corridor of Cheyyar 
SIPCOT Phase – I for “Formation of Link Road Connectivity from Valayakaranai to Manampathy”.

The plan of the lands are kept in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer (LA), Highways, Kancheepuram 
and Special Tahsildar (LA), Highways Unit- 5, Kancheepuram may be inspected on any day during office hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
69
(LA- V(1)/12122558/2025)
No. VI(1)/633(a-12)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be acquired 
for Highways Department for the purpose to “Widening from Intermediate Lane to Four Lane and Strengthening 
at Km 0/0 – 2/2 of GNT Road to Chinnambedu Road (Via) Chinnambedu Colony and Km 2/2 – 3/0 of New 
Alternative Road (PP Road – Pettai)” in Chinnambedu I, II & III Villages, Ponneri Taluk of Tiruvallur District and it 
having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the 
funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer (C & M), Tiruvallur after having considering the cause shown 
by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following 
notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 52171 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for “Widening from Intermediate Lane to Four Lane and 
Strengthening at Km 0/0 – 2/2 of GNT Road to Chinnambedu Road (Via) Chinnambedu Colony and Km 2/2 – 3/0 
of New Alternative Road (PP Road – Pettai)” at Chinnambedu I, II & III Villages, Ponneri Taluk of Tiruvallur District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer, (LA-1) Highways, Tiruvallur and in 
the office of the Special Tahsildar (LA), Highways, Unit – I, Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.
